# `ssa-nomerge` Binaryen Parity

This page is the current local signoff tracker.
Use the strategy and shape pages in this folder for the upstream Binaryen algorithm itself; use `[./implementation-structure-and-tests.md](./implementation-structure-and-tests.md)` for owner-file and proof-surface navigation. This page is about the repo's current evidence and remaining gaps.

## Durable Conclusions

- The June 2026 exceptional-edge corruption family is fixed in-tree by making HOT `ssa-nomerge` fail closed on `try_table` / throw-family flow, matching the documented SSA v1 normal-flow-only contract.
- The June 2026 default-local branchy-control drift family is fixed in the raw no-write path: reads of never-written body locals are materialized as explicit type defaults across block/loop/if/try_table bodies without invoking HOT SSA.
- The June 2026 final-lane dropped-unreachable-debris drift family is fixed in the same no-write raw path: `drop (unreachable)` / nested dropped-unreachable debris before a hard `unreachable` is collapsed using the existing shared cleanup helper.
- The April `2026-04-10` dead-param-write parity family is now fixed in-tree for `ssa-nomerge`.
- Current source-mode `ssa-nomerge` replay on the checked-in debug CLI artifact completes and validates, but exact normalized/canonical artifact equality is not currently claimed; the latest direct replay now clears the former `defined=161 abs=188` one-param br_table/decref arm call-spill first diff by spilling loaded branch payloads across following calls before a `local.tee`, and now first-diffs at `defined=215 abs=242`.
- Random compare fuzz is still useful, but it is not sufficient as the only signoff lane for `ssa-nomerge`.
- The 2026-05-07 current-head local-declaration shaping drift family is fixed in-tree: `ssa_destroy` now matches Binaryen temp-local preservation/reuse for unreachable dead `local.tee` value-if carriers without generic lowerer trimming.
- Fresh post-merge reruns on seed `0x51a` stayed clean in both the mixed-generator and `gen-valid` lanes.
- The reduced unreachable compare-carrier slice behind the traced `Func 523` family is now covered in-tree in both lift and pass tests.
- The old traced `Func 523` `writeback-validate:type mismatch` skip is now retired by the focused extracted-function CLI replay test.
- Exact raw-byte parity is still not claimed because Starshine's raw lowering path can still fail closed on artifact-only writeback families, and this follow-up did not rerun a fresh full-artifact traced skip census.
- The non-current subtype/result block-exit edge clusters now have source-backed coverage for `br_on_non_null` tested-payload widening (`ref.i31` to non-null `eqref`, child-to-parent struct/array producers, and child-to-parent `ref.func` producers) and for `br_on_null` prefix-payload widening (`ref.i31` to nullable `eqref`, child-to-parent struct/array producers, and child-to-parent `ref.func` producers); no behavior-code widening was needed beyond the existing raw branch copy lowering, spill helper, and reference matcher.

## Current In-Tree Status

- The implementation lives in `[../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge.mbt](../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge.mbt)`.
- The analysis bridge toward Binaryen `SSAify.cpp` lives in `[../../../../../src/ir/local_graph.mbt](../../../../../src/ir/local_graph.mbt)`. The 2026-06-13 `[SSA-LG]001` through `[SSA-LG]005` slices add query facts for parameter-entry sources, body-local default-entry sources, defaultability of body-local entry sources, single-source gets, multi-source merge gets, explicit write opcode kind (`local.set` versus `local.tee`), written local ids, influenced get lists, Binaryen-style already-SSA local classification, per-write merge-influence detection, and per-write no-merge freshening eligibility. `[SSANM-002a]` consumes those facts in `SsaNoMergeRewritePlan`; `[SSANM-003a]` makes the observable straight-line raw `local.set` path consume that plan for set/get freshening decisions; `[SSANM-003b]` extends the same planned straight-line path to `local.tee` while preserving tee stack results; `[SSANM-004a]` consumes planned `MaterializeDefault` get decisions for straight-line defaults plus a narrow normal structured-control subset with body-local default reads and other writes; `[SSANM-005a]` / `[SSANM-005b1]` / `[SSANM-005b2]` preserve simple one-arm, both-arm/block-`br_if`, and void-loop direct-`br_if` merge regions as canonical-only LocalGraph plans; `[SSANM-005c1]` / `[SSANM-005c2]` classify and mutate a narrow mixed fresh/canonical normal `if`/`local.set` family; `[SSANM-005c3a]` extends that mixed path to small supported `local.tee` write sets while preserving tee stack results; `[SSANM-005c3b]` classifies mixed `br_if` early exits as supported by the same planned path while keeping plain `br` and `br_table` fail-closed; and `[SSANM-005c3c]` classifies nested normal `block` / `if` as supported while keeping loops fail-closed. Plain `br` / `br_table` merge policy, broader branch/table structured-control mutation, EH, typed-control, huge-function, artifact, and preset work remain open in later `SSANM` slices. `[SSA-FULL]001` first made the sibling full `ssa` name explicit so future full-SSA work could not silently alias to this pass. `[SSA-FULL]002A` added the full-`ssa` merge planner, and `[SSA-FULL]002B` now activates `ssa` only for direct non-merge families while leaving merge-local mutation open.
- The current raw-lowering fixes live in `[../../../../../src/passes/pass_manager.mbt](../../../../../src/passes/pass_manager.mbt)`: dead param writes spill through fresh locals, live straight-line and typed-if param flows stay on the canonical param slot, no-write default-local reads are rewritten through a dedicated recursive default materializer instead of falling back to HOT SSA, no-write dropped-unreachable debris is cleaned before hard `unreachable` tails, concrete `br_on_null` taken edges insert canonical alias copies before exiting over fallthrough overwrites, concrete `br_on_non_null` exits insert canonical alias copies on the non-null taken edge when needed, no-copy `br_on_cast` / `br_on_cast_fail` exits can stay on the raw path, copy-needing non-loop cast exits, including multi-result label targets, lower through scratch source refs plus inner inverse cast-branch blocks so canonical alias copies run only on the taken edge, single-param typed-loop direct scalar `br`, all-current-target, non-current/nested all-loop-target, and source-backed mixed current-loop/enclosing-label `br_table`, no-copy or copy-needing scalar/reference `br_if` backedges, and no-copy or copy-needing nullable-reference `br_on_null` backedges use a void-loop/proxy-value-block scratch lowering, multi-param/no-result and single-result typed-loop direct current-loop `br`, `br_if`, all-current-target and non-current/nested all-loop-target `br_table`, source-backed mixed current-loop/enclosing-label `br_table` in the store model, `local.get`-, `local.tee`-, `ref.null`-, `ref.cast`-, `any.convert_extern`-, `extern.convert_any`-, `ref.i31`-, `ref.func`-, `struct.new_default`-, or `array.new_default`-tested `br_on_null`, `local.get`-, `local.tee`-, `ref.null`-, `ref.cast`-, `ref.i31`-, `ref.func`-, or module-context subtype-compatible direct `struct.new_default` / `array.new_default`-tested `br_on_non_null` (with concrete `ref.func` heap types also admitted into abstract or nominal function supertypes), and cast `br_on_cast` / `br_on_cast_fail` backedges use a scratch-per-param void-loop/store lowering, with `br_on_null` inserting loop-header canonical alias copies only in the null/taken arm, `br_on_non_null` inserting them only in the non-null/taken arm, and cast branches using inverse cast blocks so copies stay branch-local when needed; those direct current-loop backedges may also sit inside branch-bearing nested `loop` bodies when every nested branch still targets the enclosing typed loop, and may coexist with intervening nested void-loop self-target `br` / `br_if` / all-self-target `br_table` control that stays local to that inner loop, while branch-bearing no-exception nested `try_table` bodies are admitted only for the multi-param/no-result and single-result store model, and scalar proxy `try_table`, throwing/call-bearing `try_table`, non-void nested loop self-backedges, and nested branches to other labels remain fail-closed; single-reference-param loop-target `br_on_non_null` backedges use the same void-loop/proxy-value-block lowering as loop-target casts, and copy-needing single-reference-param loop-target cast backedges lower through inverse cast blocks that store the cast payload into the loop scratch and run branch-specific canonical alias copies before the void backedge.
- That rule is an in-tree inference from Binaryen `src/passes/SSAify.cpp` `createNewIndexes()` plus direct `wasm-opt --ssa-nomerge` micro-replays on reduced param-write cases.
- The same pass-manager path still rejects per-function writebacks that fail module-aware validation, in addition to the existing `invalid-escape-carrier` and `suspicious-escape-carrier` families.
- The `cmd` package contains a native debug-artifact replay test in `[../../../../../src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt](../../../../../src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt)`, and a focused `moon test src/cmd --target native --filter 'run_cmd_with_adapter validates ssa-nomerge on debug artifact'` run is currently green.
- The reduced `Func 523` follow-up now also lives in `[../../../../../src/ir/hot_lift.mbt](../../../../../src/ir/hot_lift.mbt)`, `[../../../../../src/ir/hot_lift_test.mbt](../../../../../src/ir/hot_lift_test.mbt)`, `[../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt](../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt)`, and the focused extracted-function CLI replay in `[../../../../../src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt](../../../../../src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt)`.
- The 2026-06-09 audit added focused `try_table` exceptional-exit, branchy default-local-read, dropped-unreachable-debris, nested param-slot, large structured raw coverage, needed-only branch/label copies, canonical body-local writes, and `Func 4302` carrier-narrowing regressions in `[../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt](../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt)`; details and command evidence live in `[../../../raw/research/0722-2026-06-09-ssa-nomerge-exceptional-edge-audit.md](../../../raw/research/0722-2026-06-09-ssa-nomerge-exceptional-edge-audit.md)`.

## Current Signoff State

- 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-005c3b]` / `[SSANM-005c3c]` mixed branch and nested-control classification: `src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` now has focused public-pipeline coverage proving the current narrow mixed-region gate boundaries. `ssa-nomerge LocalGraph freshens mixed br_if early-exit writes` proves a mixed region with an early `br_if 0` uses `structured-mixed-localgraph-plan`: the pre-merge write is freshened to local `2`, branch-merge writes stay canonical on local `1`, and the branch remains a `br_if`. `ssa-nomerge keeps mixed plain br regions off LocalGraph path` and `ssa-nomerge keeps mixed br_table regions off LocalGraph path` prove plain `br` and `br_table` mixed regions validate but do not take the planned mixed path, preserving branch-alias/table helper ownership. `ssa-nomerge LocalGraph freshens nested mixed block if writes` proves nested normal `block` / `if` / `block` shapes use the mixed path and freshen only planned non-merge writes to locals `2` and `3`; `ssa-nomerge keeps mixed loop regions off LocalGraph path` proves loop-containing mixed regions remain fail-closed for later structured-control / typed-loop owners. Red-first was not practical because this classification slice documents/protects existing gate behavior rather than changing mutation. Final evidence so far: focused `moon test --package jtenner/starshine/passes --file ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `402/402`. Direct compare was not required because no pass behavior changed; the last behavior-changing mixed-region slice remains `[SSANM-005c3a]` below. Agent classification: supported mixed normal-control now covers `local.set`, small `local.tee`, `br_if` early exits, and nested normal `block` / `if`; plain `br`, `br_table`, loops, EH, typed control, huge-function/artifact classification, and dedicated GenValid profile allocation mismatches stay open.

- 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-005c3a]` mixed fresh/canonical `local.tee` admission: `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` now lets the existing `structured-mixed-localgraph-plan` path handle small supported normal-control mixed regions that contain `local.tee` writes. The planned structured rewrite cursor already knew how to retarget tee writes; this slice narrows the gate so tee-bearing mixed regions with at most four local writes can use it, while larger tee-heavy artifact scratch/copy families continue through existing helpers. The focused public-pipeline fixture in `src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` proves freshenable tee writes are retargeted to planned locals `2` and `3`, the tee stack result is preserved through a final `i32.add`, both merge-feeding `local.set`s and the merge read stay canonical on local `1`, no predecessor-copy merge local is introduced, and the trace reason is `structured-mixed-localgraph-plan`. Red-first evidence: the new fixture initially failed because the legacy path kept only the original body local. Final evidence: `moon fmt`; `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings; focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `397/397`; `moon test src/passes` passed `2427/2427`; full `moon test` passed `5732/5732`; native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` completed with pre-existing pass-manager unused-function warnings; and direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-ssanm005c3a-tee-10000` requested `10000`, compared `7601`, had `7601` normalized matches, `0` cleanup-normalized matches, `0` mismatches, `0` validation/property/generator failures, `20` Binaryen/tool command failures (`19` `binaryen-rec-group-zero`, `1` `binaryen-bad-section-size`), and cache hits (`wasm-smith` `3811/0`, Binaryen `7601/0`, Binaryen failures `20/0`). Agent classification at the time: no raw mismatch family was introduced in the mixed-generator direct lane; `[SSANM-005c3b]` / `[SSANM-005c3c]` later classified mixed `br_if` and nested normal `block` / `if` coverage while keeping plain `br`, `br_table`, loops, EH/typed-control boundaries, huge-function/artifact classification, and dedicated GenValid profile allocation mismatches open.

- 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-005c1]` / `[SSANM-005c2]` mixed fresh/canonical merge-region classification and narrow mutation: `src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` now has a focused mixed-plan fixture showing that one original body local can have two freshenable `local.set` writes around a canonical both-arm merge region: the LocalGraph plan reports two `Freshen` writes, two canonical merge-feeding writes, two retargeted gets, and one canonical merge get. `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` now admits a narrow normal structured-control family without `local.tee`, branch exits, loops, `br_table`, `br_on_*`, cast branches, or EH: when the plan has mixed fresh/canonical merge decisions, it recursively applies planned freshening/retargeting and returns `structured-mixed-localgraph-plan`. The public-pipeline fixture proves the early and post-merge `local.set`s are retargeted to planned locals `2` and `3`, both-arm merge-feeding writes plus the merge read stay on canonical local `1`, no predecessor-copy merge local is introduced, and output validation remains green. Red-first evidence: the classification test first failed on the missing mixed-plan summary helper, and the public-pipeline fixture then failed because the current path kept only the original body local. Final evidence: `moon fmt`; focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `396/396`; `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings; `moon test src/passes` passed `2426/2426`; full `moon test` passed `5731/5731`; native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` completed with pre-existing pass-manager unused-function warnings; and direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-ssanm005c2-mixed-10000` requested `10000`, compared `7605`, had `7605` normalized matches, `0` cleanup-normalized matches, `0` mismatches, `0` validation/property/generator failures, `20` Binaryen/tool command failures (`19` `binaryen-rec-group-zero`, `1` `binaryen-bad-section-size`), and cache hits (`wasm-smith` `3813/0`, Binaryen `7605/0`, Binaryen failures `20/0`). Agent classification at the time: no raw mismatch family was introduced in the mixed-generator direct lane; `[SSANM-005c3a]` later admitted small `local.tee`, and `[SSANM-005c3b]` / `[SSANM-005c3c]` later classified mixed `br_if` plus nested normal `block` / `if`. Plain `br`, `br_table`, loops, EH/typed-control boundaries, huge-function/artifact classification, and dedicated GenValid profile allocation mismatches remain open for later SSANM slices.

- 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-005b2]` loop/backedge canonical merge preservation: `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` now recognizes a narrow void-loop family where a direct `br_if 0` backedge participates in a canonical-only LocalGraph no-merge plan. The raw dispatcher checks this family before the legacy `run_hot_pipeline_raw_ssa_nomerge_should_defer_loop_carried_br_if_to_hot(...)` HOT defer, and returns unchanged with trace reason `structured-loop-backedge-merge-localgraph-plan` when a multi-source merge get is fed only by canonical writes. The path deliberately admits only simple void loops with direct body `br_if 0`; it rejects typed loops, nested blocks/loops, plain `br`, `br_table`, `br_on_*`, cast branches, and `try_table`, so existing typed-loop/value-backedge scratch lowerings and branch-alias helpers remain active for their boundary tests. The updated public-pipeline fixture in `src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` proves the entry write and backedge write stay on canonical local `0`, both reads stay on local `0`, no temp or predecessor-copy local is introduced, and the LocalGraph loop-backedge trace fires. Red-first evidence: the focused test initially failed because the legacy path still added scratch locals (`3` i32 locals instead of `1`). Final evidence: `moon fmt`; focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `394/394`; `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings; `moon test src/passes` passed `2424/2424`; full `moon test` passed `5729/5729`; native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` completed with pre-existing pass-manager unused-function warnings; `git diff --check` passed; and direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-ssanm005b2-loop-backedge-10000` requested `10000`, compared `7607`, had `7607` normalized matches, `0` cleanup-normalized matches, `0` mismatches, `0` validation/property/generator failures, `20` Binaryen/tool command failures (`19` `binaryen-rec-group-zero`, `1` `binaryen-bad-section-size`), and cache hits (`wasm-smith` `3814/0`, Binaryen `7607/0`, Binaryen failures `20/0`). Agent classification: no raw mismatch family was introduced in the mixed-generator direct lane; nested loop/control backedges, plain `br` / `br_table` policy, mixed per-write structured regions, structured tee/control mutation, EH/typed-control boundaries, huge-function/artifact classification, and dedicated GenValid profile allocation mismatches stay open.

- 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-005b1]` simple multi-source merge preservation: `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` now recognizes a narrow normal structured-control family where the LocalGraph rewrite plan is canonical-only and a merge get has multiple reaching sources from merge-feeding writes. Those functions trace `structured-multisource-merge-localgraph-plan` and return unchanged instead of invoking the legacy structured local-write rewriter, so simple both-arm `if` writes and block/`br_if` early-exit merges cannot gain fresh merge locals or predecessor copies. Focused public-pipeline tests in `src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` prove both merge-feeding writes stay on local `1`, the final get stays on local `1`, and only the original body local remains. That `[SSANM-005b1]` path deliberately excludes loops/backedges, plain `br`, `br_table`, `br_on_*`, cast branches, and `try_table` because existing typed-control/branch-alias lowerings needed separate classification. Red-first evidence: both new fixtures initially failed because the trace still reported `structured-local-writes`. Final evidence: `moon fmt`; focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `394/394`; `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings; `moon test src/passes` passed `2424/2424`; full `moon test` passed `5729/5729`; native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` completed with pre-existing pass-manager unused-function warnings; `git diff --check` passed; and direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-ssanm005b1-multisource-merge-10000` requested `10000`, compared `7607`, had `7607` normalized matches, `0` cleanup-normalized matches, `0` mismatches, `0` validation/property/generator failures, `20` Binaryen/tool command failures (`19` `binaryen-rec-group-zero`, `1` `binaryen-bad-section-size`), and cache hits (`wasm-smith` `3814/0`, Binaryen `7607/0`, Binaryen failures `20/0`). Agent classification at the time: no raw mismatch family was introduced in the mixed-generator direct lane; `[SSANM-005b2]` later narrowed simple void-loop direct `br_if 0` backedges, while nested loop/control backedges, plain `br` / `br_table` policy, mixed per-write structured regions, structured tee/control mutation, EH/typed-control boundaries, huge-function/artifact classification, and dedicated GenValid profile allocation mismatches stay open.

- 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-005a]` one-arm entry/default merge preservation: `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` now recognizes the narrow missing-else structured-control family where the LocalGraph rewrite plan is canonical-only and a merge get sees exactly one explicit write plus the matching entry/default source. Those functions trace `structured-one-arm-merge-localgraph-plan` and return unchanged rather than invoking the legacy structured local-write rewriter, so no fresh merge local or predecessor copy can be introduced for the one-arm body-local/default and parameter-entry cases. Focused public-pipeline tests in `src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` prove a body-local default merge keeps `local.set 1` plus final `local.get 1` with only the original body local, and a parameter-entry merge keeps `local.set 0` plus final `local.get 0` with no appended locals. The path deliberately excludes loops, `br_table`, `br_on_*`, cast branches, and `try_table`; those remain in `[SSANM-005b]`, `[SSANM-006a]`, and `[SSANM-007*]`. Red-first evidence: both new one-arm fixtures initially failed because the trace still reported `structured-local-writes`. Final evidence: `moon fmt`; `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings; focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `392/392`; `moon test src/passes` passed `2422/2422`; full `moon test` passed `5727/5727`; native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` completed with pre-existing pass-manager unused-function warnings; `git diff --check` passed; and direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-ssanm005a-one-arm-merge-10000` requested `10000`, compared `7602`, had `7602` normalized matches, `0` cleanup-normalized matches, `0` mismatches, `0` validation/property/generator failures, `20` Binaryen/tool command failures (`19` `binaryen-rec-group-zero`, `1` `binaryen-bad-section-size`), and cache hits (`wasm-smith` `3811/0`, Binaryen `7602/0`, Binaryen failures `20/0`). Agent classification: no raw mismatch family was introduced in the mixed-generator direct lane; at that point broader both-arm/multi-source merges, per-write mixed structured regions, structured tee/control mutation, EH/typed-control boundaries, huge-function/artifact classification, and dedicated GenValid profile allocation mismatches stayed open. `[SSANM-005b1]` later narrowed the both-arm/block-`br_if` subset and `[SSANM-005b2]` narrowed simple void-loop direct-`br_if` backedges, while nested loop/control backedges and branch-table merge policy remain open.

- 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-004b]` no-write default fast-path narrowing: `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` no longer has a separate recursive raw default-only rewriter for no-local-write functions. The no-write path now builds the same `SsaNoMergeRewritePlan` as the LocalGraph mutation paths and runs `run_hot_pipeline_raw_ssa_nomerge_materialize_default_func(...)` when the plan contains legal `MaterializeDefault` get decisions. Dropped-unreachable-debris cleanup remains a separate no-write fast path and can still rewrite a no-local-write function without asking the default plan to make a change. Focused public-pipeline tests in `src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` prove a branchy no-write `br_table` default read now traces `default-local-reads-localgraph-plan` while still replacing the body-local read with `i32.const 0`, and a no-write dropped-unreachable fixture still traces `no-local-writes-unreachable-debris` with the block/drop debris removed. Red-first evidence: the branchy default fixture initially failed because the trace still reported the legacy `default-local-reads` reason. Final evidence: `moon fmt`; focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `390/390`; `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings; `moon test src/passes` passed `2420/2420`; full `moon test` passed `5725/5725`; native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` completed with pre-existing pass-manager unused-function warnings; `git diff --check` passed; and direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-ssanm004b-default-fastpath-10000` requested `10000`, compared `7604`, had `7604` normalized matches, `0` cleanup-normalized matches, `0` mismatches, `0` validation/property/generator failures, `20` Binaryen/tool command failures (`19` `binaryen-rec-group-zero`, `1` `binaryen-bad-section-size`), and cache hits (`wasm-smith` `3812/0`, Binaryen `7604/0`, Binaryen failures `20/0`). Agent classification: this slice removed duplicated default-local rewrite policy without introducing any raw mismatch family in the mixed-generator direct lane; multi-source merge defaults, broader structured mutation, EH/typed-control boundaries, and dedicated GenValid profile allocation mismatches stay open for later SSANM slices.

- 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-004a]` LocalGraph default-entry get materialization: `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` now reuses `SsaNoMergeRewritePlan` `MaterializeDefault` get decisions beyond the old no-local-write raw special case. - 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-003b]` LocalGraph straight-line `local.tee` mutation: `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` no longer diverts straight-line functions containing `local.tee` to the legacy alias heuristic. The raw straight-line path now consumes `SsaNoMergeRewritePlan` for both `local.set` and `local.tee`: planned `Freshen` tee writes allocate the next planned body local and rewrite the tee target to that local, planned canonical tee writes keep the original local, and planned gets still retarget/materialize/keep according to the LocalGraph get decision. - 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-011a]` GenValid profile and feature-label inventory: the current in-tree SSA generator family has four profile spellings. `ssa-nomerge-smoke` is the quick structured-local profile, `ssa-nomerge-coverage` and `ssa-nomerge-stress` are dense profiles, `ssa-nomerge-parity` is narrower but is **not currently compare-clean**, and the alias `ssa-nomerge` resolves to `ssa-nomerge-coverage`. The profile configs share Binaryen-oracle coverage-forced defaults with imports/memories/tables/globals/tags/ref-types/v128/calls disabled, `allow_ssa_nomerge_body_generator=true`, branch-heavy control enabled, and max locals of `8` for parity, `10` for smoke, and `12` for coverage/stress. Existing source/tests already prove the profile names, seed `0x5eed` feature facts, feature-floor labels, and batch selection helper.

  | LocalGraph decision-table area | Existing feature labels / facts | Current profile coverage | Follow-up owner |
  | --- | --- | --- | --- |
  | Already-SSA / single-source straight-line writes | `ssa-straight-line-local-chain`, `ssa-already-ssa-local`, `ssa-multi-def-same-local`, `ssa-param-entry-read`, `ssa-param-write`, `ssa-dead-local-set` | parity, smoke, coverage, stress | `[SSANM-011b]` added explicit already-SSA and parameter-entry labels/floors. |

Non-current explicit-operand call inputs, call_ref/return_call_ref inputs, multi-result calls, and operandful aggregate/data forms remain fail-closed or open as documented below.

- 2026-06-12 zero-param call `br_on_non_null` follow-up: raw structured `ssa-nomerge` now admits the narrow problem-1 subset where a zero-param, single-reference-result `call` feeds a current typed-loop store-model `br_on_non_null`. The helper infers the call result type from `HotModuleContext`, spills the already-evaluated call result once into a defaultable scratch, and reuses the existing non-null loop-store branch lowering; it deliberately does not scan backward over arbitrary call operands. Red evidence: `ssa-nomerge rewrites problem1 zero-param call br_on_non_null loop-store input` initially failed with HOT lift `UnsupportedInstruction((br_on_non_null (Label 0)))`; after the narrow raw-gate and spill-helper change, focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `286/286`, `moon test src/passes` passed `2307/2307`, `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings, full `moon test` passed `5582/5582`, native `src/cmd` build passed with pre-existing warnings, and direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-zero-param-call-10000-rerun` requested `10000`, compared `7603`, had `7603` normalized matches, `0` mismatches, and `20` Binaryen/tool command failures. - 2026-06-12 problem-1 arbitrary reference-input coverage slice: added executable coverage for the remaining arbitrary multi-instruction reference branch-input breadth without widening unsafe expression scanning. Positive-supported coverage now explicitly distinguishes typed `if` / typed `select` / direct typed producers from unsupported arbitrary expressions. The guard contract is output validation plus raw branch preservation; some shapes reach HOT and are rejected by writeback validation. - 2026-06-12 sampled debug-artifact local-allocation parity refresh: the saved `.tmp/self-ssa-nomerge-debug-wasi-bronull-prefix-subtype-results` first-diff bucket was refreshed after native artifact generation was unblocked by commit `e0f786434`, then reduced through commits `0dc102965` and `ee4a17d0e`. The `abs=111` typed loop-param shape was a real parity gap: Binaryen lowered the loop-carried scalar through a fresh scratch while Starshine kept the typed loop. That gap is now covered by `ssa-nomerge artifact parity lowers loop-param block-branch scratch` in `src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt`, and refreshed Starshine output writes the loop-param scratch while keeping Binaryen-like canonical pre-loop/header tees. The residual sampled differences at `abs=95`, `abs=98`, `abs=110`, `abs=111`, and `abs=115` are classified as Starshine-winning differences, not uninspected representation drift: inspected residuals are dominated by Starshine keeping single-use call results on the Wasm operand stack across intervening void calls instead of spilling and immediately reloading extra locals. This is semantically safe because the intervening void calls consume only their explicit operands and cannot observe the lower stack value; if they trap, the spill/local state is unobservable. Refreshed current metrics show smaller canonical print/body text and fewer local writes/gets for every sampled residual: `abs=95` Binaryen `print=140614 body=114259 locals=1090 writes=929 gets=1847 maxref=1089` versus Starshine `print=128849 body=108952 locals=822 writes=819 gets=1741 maxref=821`; `abs=98` Binaryen `18203/14697/140/121/245/139` versus Starshine `17091/13857/126/103/226/125`; `abs=110` Binaryen `28141/22116/247/204/307/246` versus Starshine `26810/21083/232/181/280/231`; `abs=111` Binaryen `6286/4916/51/41/69/50` versus Starshine `6206/4828/49/39/67/48`; and `abs=115` Binaryen `10189/8950/46/37/132/45` versus Starshine `10043/8818/43/34/129/42`. This classification is artifact-sample scoped: it does not claim exact artifact equality, final pass closeout, or that future local-allocation drift can be waved through without the same semantic and measurement evidence.

- 2026-06-12 prefix-payload if-result `br_on_non_null` follow-up: raw structured `ssa-nomerge` now preserves non-current block-exit prefix label payloads when the final tested reference is a trailing single-result `if (result ref)` feeding `br_on_non_null`. The red repro used a block result `(i32, externref)`: the `i32` prefix was already on the stack after spilling the tested ref, and the old synthetic `ref.is_null` / else-branch rewrite failed validation with `writeback-validate:stack underflow`. The fix spills only prefix label results (all label result lanes before the final tested ref) around the synthetic `if`, restores them in the non-null/taken branch before `ref.as_non_null`, and restores them on the null fallthrough so the original fallthrough producer can still supply the final nullable ref. This is Binaryen behavior Starshine should implement: no raw `br_on_non_null` remains after the effectful typed-`if` producer, and output validates without duplicating branch condition or arm effects. Broader arbitrary multi-instruction inputs, type-indexed/multi-result producers, multi-result typed loops, `try_table`, nested non-void/other-target branches, exact artifact parity, and O4z slot policy remain active.

Starshine pass-local time was `26.731 ms` versus Binaryen `392.500 ms`, and final direct output size is now size-winning for Starshine (`3150432` bytes versus Binaryen `3155990`). `bun validate self-opt-smoke --wasm .tmp/self-ssa-nomerge-debug-wasi-canonical-local/starshine.wasm --limit 1` validated the artifact and completed with `0` failures.

## Coverage / Investigation Lanes

### 2026-06-09 join-allocation investigation (case `000001`)

Reduced block-join replay (`.tmp/ssa-block-join-minimal/`) proves **semantic-equivalent join allocation drift** when both tools actually run `ssa-nomerge`: Starshine’s raw structured path keeps canonical slots (`$x`/`$x`/`$x`) while Binaryen fresh-allocates per set (`$2`/`$3`/`$3`). Both outputs validate and observe the same post-join value.

The dense GenValid `ssa-nomerge` profile smoke lane (`0/100` normalized) is **not** primarily a normalizer gap. For case `000001`, `starshine.raw.wasm` is unchanged from input (`330` bytes, HOT `changed=false`, raw structured rewrite `None`), while Binaryen applies `--ssa-nomerge` (`271` bytes). The harness compares canonicalized **untransformed** Starshine output against Binaryen’s transformed output because the dense template combines fail-closed / raw-skip shapes with rewrite-expected slices in one function (`ssa_nested_cfg_fail_closed_shape`, dropped-increment guard shapes, and combined structured density).

**Classification:** coverage-lane artifact for the dense profile; `semantic-equivalent-join-allocation-drift` only for isolated fixtures where both sides transform.

**Normalizer:** opt-in `--normalize ssa-local-allocation-debris` stays narrow (straight-line islands and immediate pre-`if` carriers only). Do not broaden it across control-flow joins without proof and negative tests.

**Signoff baseline:** mixed-generator `100000` lane with `--normalize local-cleanup-debris` (`99751/99751` normalized matches) under **Current Signoff State** above.

### GenValid profile split (2026-06-09)

| Profile | Purpose | Templates included | Templates excluded |
|---|---|---|---|
| `ssa-nomerge-coverage` (`ssa-nomerge` alias) | Dense SSA body templates, all `ssa-*` coverage floors, fail-closed stress shapes, supported nested `drop(if (result t) ...)` family | straight-line multi-def, tee, param write, if-join, default merge, loop backedge, typed loop-param/backedge fail-closed, `try_table`/`throw_ref` exceptional fail-closed, block join, br_table, parallel-copy (+ cycle), unreachable carrier, dropped increment guarded/reversed, dropped-unreachable debris before hard unreachable, nested-CFG fail-closed, nested result-if straight-line/scalar/condition/arm/mixed templates, structured early-return, block `br`/`br_if`, structured-param merge, branch-local-not-read-later, default-local read after branchy control, canonical body-local next-read, immediate `local.set; br` block exit, enclosing-label copy-before-exit, void br_table canonical copies | — |
| `ssa-nomerge-smoke` | Quick coverage-signal profile for smoke/regression runs that should hit structured SSA branch shapes without dense stress slices | straight-line multi-def, tee, param write (when i32 param), if-join phi, one-arm default merge, structured early-return, block `br`/`br_if`, structured-param merge, branch-local-not-read-later, default-local read after branchy control, canonical body-local next-read, immediate `local.set; br` block exit, enclosing-label copy-before-exit | loop backedge, br_table (including void br_table copy dispatch), parallel-copy, unreachable carrier, dropped increment guarded/reversed, dropped-unreachable debris before hard unreachable, nested-CFG / typed-loop / exceptional fail-closed, dense nested result-if condition/value-block/scalar variants |
| `ssa-nomerge-parity` | Green compare candidate: rewrite shapes where both tools transform without fail-closed skip or structured branch allocation drift | straight-line multi-def, tee, param write (when i32 param), if-join phi, one-arm default merge | loop backedge, block join, br_table, parallel-copy, unreachable carrier, dropped increment guarded/reversed, dropped-unreachable debris, nested-CFG / typed-loop / exceptional fail-closed, nested result-if coverage templates, structured branch smoke shapes, default-local branchy-control, canonical-next-read, immediate set/br, enclosing-label copy-before-exit, and void br_table copy structured slices |
| `ssa-nomerge-stress` | Reserved pathological/fail-closed lane (currently aliases dense coverage templates) | same as coverage (including typed-loop-param, exceptional-flow, and nested result-if templates) | — |

Use `--gen-valid-profile ssa-nomerge-parity` with parity-appropriate `--require-feature` floors for targeted green GenValid parity-profile compare lanes. Use `--gen-valid-profile ssa-nomerge-smoke` when a quick smoke should hit structured branch SSA coverage and tolerate current local-allocation representation drift. Keep `--gen-valid-profile ssa-nomerge-coverage` (or legacy `ssa-nomerge`) for dense scanner/floor coverage only. The broad mixed-generator `100000` lane with `--normalize local-cleanup-debris` remains the primary signoff baseline; a green parity-profile lane is strong targeted evidence, not a replacement for that baseline.

2026-06-09 parity-profile compare (trimmed templates A–E only, `--normalize ssa-local-allocation-debris --normalize local-cleanup-debris`):

- `100/100` compared, `100` compare-normalized matches, `0` mismatches (`.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-profile-100-v2`)
- `1000/1000` compared, `1000` compare-normalized matches, `0` mismatches (`.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-profile-1000`)
- `10000/10000` compared, `10000` compare-normalized matches, `0` mismatches (`.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-profile-10000`)

These lanes are **targeted GenValid SSA parity-profile signoff** for the trimmed template set. They do not replace the broad mixed-generator `99751/100000` signoff baseline above.

The earlier dense-profile smoke (`ssa-nomerge-coverage` with loop/block/br_table/parallel-copy in one function) and the quick `ssa-nomerge-smoke` structured-branch lane remain coverage-lane artifacts, not parity-profile compare lanes, until the compare normalizer or pass output converges for structured control-flow local allocation. Current 2026-06-11 smoke evidence: `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-smoke-profile-100` requested and compared `100/100`, with `0` validation/generator/command failures and `100` expected local-allocation representation mismatches. A later branch-copy narrowing run `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-smoke-branch-copy-100` still compares `100/100` with `100` representation mismatches and no validation/generator/command failures; case `000001` writes the unconditional block-exit `local.set; br` path directly to the canonical merge slot. The local-tee/no-copy-`br_if` slice preserves no-copy `br_if` in the focused fixtures and keeps the paired GenValid parity lane green (`.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-tee-brif-genvalid-normalized-1000`, `1000` compare-normalized matches, `0` mismatches), while `ssa-nomerge-smoke` remains dirty (`.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-smoke-tee-brif-genvalid-normalized-100`, `100/100` mismatches) because broader structured allocation drift remains. The paired green parity checks `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-profile-100-post-smoke` and `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-branch-copy-100` each compared `100/100` with `100` compare-normalized matches and `0` mismatches.

2026-06-11 deeper GenValid SSA coverage adds positive coverage/stress specimens for the previously scanner-only fail-closed facts: `ssa-typed-loop-param-fail-closed-shape` now comes from a valid typed loop-param/backedge template, and `ssa-exceptional-fail-closed-shape` now comes from a valid `try_table` + `throw_ref` template with local writes. These remain coverage/stress-only and are intentionally excluded from `ssa-nomerge-parity` and `ssa-nomerge-smoke`; they prove generator/scanner/floor coverage, not pass closeout.

2026-06-11 raw structured GenValid widening adds four more facts from the recent pass-behavior slices: `ssa-default-local-read-after-branchy-control`, `ssa-dropped-unreachable-debris-before-hard-unreachable`, `ssa-canonical-body-local-next-read`, and `ssa-immediate-block-exit-canonical-set-br`. Coverage/stress include all four; smoke includes the three quick structured allocation signals and intentionally excludes dropped-unreachable debris; parity remains the conservative A–E set. A later same-day copy-family widening adds `ssa-enclosing-label-copy-before-exit` and `ssa-void-br-table-canonical-copies`; coverage/stress include both, smoke includes only the quick enclosing-label copy signal, and parity still excludes both. The coverage/stress/smoke required-feature compare lanes are intentionally dirty but validate and generate without command failures; the parity profile stayed green at `1000/1000` in `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-new-copy-facts-genvalid-normalized-1000-final`.

2026-06-10 nested result-if GenValid coverage (templates O–W in `gen_valid_ssa.mbt`, feature facts `ssa-nested-result-if-*`):

- New GenValid facts distinguish supported `drop(if (result t) ...)` shapes from `ssa-nested-cfg-fail-closed-shape` (`drop(block (result t) ...)` with local writes).
- `ssa-nested-result-if-supported-shape` means the scanner matched the supported `ssa_simple_drop_result_if_allowed(...)` family: stack-boundary condition-window detection (not whole-function prefix), straight-line or single `block (result i32)` conditions, straight-line / single value-block / void-prefix + final value-block arms, both arms present, and scalar `i32`/`i64`/`f32`/`f64` results only. The scanner is conservative: false negatives are acceptable; false positives are not.
- Templates are wired into `ssa-nomerge-coverage` and `ssa-nomerge-stress` only; `ssa-nomerge-parity` stays on the conservative A–E template set.
- Targeted `--require-feature ssa-nested-result-if-supported-shape` lanes on the dense coverage profile are **coverage smoke**, not parity signoff: they combine rewrite-expected nested result-if slices with fail-closed / join-allocation drift shapes in one function body. A dirty 100-case lane is expected when allocation drift and fail-closed shapes share the same dense body. Post-`bcf4b9199` smoke at `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-nested-result-if-supported-100-post-bcf4` reproduced the expected dirty lane (`100/100` mismatches, `0` command failures) with both tools transforming every case.

### 2026-06-10 large-structured skip extraction (`Func 3668` / `Func 1265`)

Post-bcf4 trace census (`.tmp/ssa-nomerge-post-bcf4-trace/stderr.txt`) had `17` `large-structured-local-writes` skips and `0` `skip-invalid-lower` lines. The smallest skip by scanned instruction count was **`Func 3668`** (`instrs=4509`, `locals=620`); the next-smallest named target was **`Func 1265`** (`instrs=4563`, `locals=614`).

**Classification:** raw structured-path **instruction-count threshold only**. In `run_hot_pipeline_raw_ssa_nomerge` (`pass_manager.mbt`), branch-bearing structured functions skipped when `instr_count > structured_branch_raw_instr_limit` (`4096`) or when `base_local_count > structured_branch_raw_local_limit` (`1024`). Both `Func 3668` and `Func 1265` exceeded the instruction limit only (`4509` / `4563` > `4096`; locals stay well under `1024`). This was not `skip-invalid-lower`, not nested-CFG HOT fail-closed, not typed-loop-param control, and not exceptional flow.

The 2026-06-11 threshold slices raised the branch-bearing structured raw instruction budget to `4608` first, then both the branch-bearing and no-branch structured instruction budgets to `5376`, after synthetic red/green boundary coverage and extracted-artifact validation for sampled functions. Fresh full-artifact trace `.tmp/ssa-nomerge-structured-8192-brtable-trace/stderr.txt` now has `9` `large-structured-local-writes` skips and `0` `skip-invalid-lower` lines. The 2026-06-11 8192-budget follow-up additionally admitted `Func 502` (`7132` / `827`) and `Func 5418` (`7925` / `894`) after red/green synthetic boundary coverage, direct compare, and full-artifact trace validation. Remaining threshold/local-count owners are `Func 265` (`9664` / `1175`), `Func 3518` (`8965` / `1547`), `Func 3536` (`16195` / `2871`), `Func 3781` (`39283` / `6634`), `Func 3885` (`26350` / `3879`), `Func 4119` (`9458` / `1332`), `Func 4522` (`12067` / `976`), `Func 5417` (`19507` / `3524`), and `Func 5419` (`15300` / `2313`).

**Extraction replay:** `--extract-functions=3668` roots a large dependency closure (`.tmp/ssa-nomerge-large-structured-func3668/extracted.wasm`, validates). The rooted function replays as `Func 24` with the same `instrs=4509 locals=620` payload and `large-structured-local-writes` trace. Starshine leaves that function unchanged on the raw fast path; Binaryen `--ssa-nomerge` transforms the extracted module. Self-opt compare on the extracted module validates both sides but is not normalized/canonical equal (`defined=1 abs=25` first diff).

**Reduced fixture:** a programmatic WAT fixture with one `block ... br 0` prefix plus `1030` `if/else` pairs crosses the same threshold (`instrs=4125`, `large-structured-local-writes`); `1020` pairs stay on `structured-local-writes` (`instrs=4085`). Regression tests in `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` lock that boundary without embedding the 1.5 MB extracted artifact.

**Next slice:** keep the 9 remaining artifact functions in backlog until measured raw-structured rewrite cost/validation evidence exists; do not raise the structured raw instruction/local budgets from a single extracted replay or without preserving direct compare and artifact validation evidence.

## Remaining Gap

- Dropped-local-increment debris no longer triggers a whole-function HOT fail-closed skip. HOT SSA rewrite preserves reaching locals for the exact `drop(i32.add(local.get, i32.const 1))` shape and `local.tee` variants on reduced HOT-path fixtures; reversed operands and non-`1` constants remain validated boundary shapes. Broader integer widths remain unclaimed until tested.
- A tiny nested-CFG subset is now supported on the HOT path: straight-line `drop(block (result t) ...)` value blocks with only local get/set/tee, constants, and simple numeric ops (`ssa_simple_drop_value_block_allowed(...)` plus inline rename in `ssa_local_visit_node`), and straight-line `drop(if (result t) ...)` with a single scalar numeric result (`i32`/`i64`/`f32`/`f64`), both arms present, and a straight-line terminator-free condition with local get/set/tee and simple numeric traffic, or one simple `block (result i32)` condition with the same straight-line local traffic (`ssa_simple_condition_value_block_allowed(...)` / `ssa_simple_result_if_condition_allowed(...)` / `ssa_simple_drop_result_if_allowed(...)` plus CFG-backed rename/use-def inline visits with per-root segment isolation and join phis on the post-`drop` continuation). Condition-local writes are allowed only because CFG keeps branch-free condition blocks in the predecessor block that dominates both arms and rename/use-def visit that block before the arm regions; branches and nested control in the condition stay fail-closed. The dropped result value is not SSA-modeled; arms still need CFG/SSA for local traffic. `v128`, reference/GC, and multi-value result-if remain unsupported. `ssa_nomerge_has_nested_cfg_sensitive_control(...)` still fail-closes all other nested value-control shapes.
- Nested CFG-sensitive behavior remains fail-closed for HOT SSA mutation beyond the supported subsets and is regression-covered: nested result-typed `if` inside dropped value blocks, nested `br` / `br_if` / `loop` / nested `if` inside supported operand shapes, missing-else or multi-value operand `if`, and broader nested control must not produce `pass[ssa-nomerge]:mutated` on the hot path and must leave the hot-path revision unchanged. Root-level value blocks and structured control bodies whose children are region-root slots remain outside this guard and may still rewrite through HOT SSA or the raw no-write path.
- Future work requires nested-region-aware liveness/use-def for unsupported shapes, exact local read discovery inside arbitrary nested value control, rename/destruction for nested `if`/loop/branch shapes, and lowering tests that prove local copies are inserted only at valid stack-neutral sites — not Binaryen parity claims for full nested CFG-sensitive SSA.
- Void loop backedges now have a narrow raw structured subset: void `loop` bodies and void loop-target `br` / `br_table` backedges can rewrite without entering HOT SSA, using loop-header read-before-write facts to preserve loop-carried canonical locals and to freshen only dead loop-local writes. This subset covers the source-backed no-copy loop-target `br_table` and loop-carried read-before-write `br_table` regressions; no-copy loop-target `br_if` is also admitted by the later conditional-backedge slice. Copy-needing conditional loop backedges, result-carrying loop targets, and broader loop-param ABI remain unsupported.
- Typed loop-param control has narrow raw structured exceptions for direct current-loop backedges. No-result single-param loops use the proxy value-block model for scalar and reference branch families; no-result multi-param loops use a scratch-per-param store model for direct `br`, `br_if`, all-current-target `br_table`, and no-copy `br_on_null` whose tested nullable ref is a lowered `local.get`; single-result loops use the same store model plus a synthetic outer result block for direct `br`, `br_if`, all-current-target `br_table`, and the same no-copy `br_on_null` subset. Multi-result typed loops, non-current-loop `br_table` targets, branch-bearing nested `loop` / `try_table` bodies, copy-needing multi-param `br_on_null`, arbitrary-tested `br_on_null`, and broader result-loop/reference `br_on_*` header models remain explicitly unsupported and intentionally fail-closed. HOT represents typed loop params as `BlockResultResolved` param prefixes on `HotOp::Loop` children and as branch operands on backedges, with `HotLabelInfo.branch_arity` recording the payload count. SSA v1's local overlay models only `LocalGet` / `LocalSet` / `LocalTee` reaching definitions; it does not treat loop-param stack flow as local defs, and destruction only inserts predecessor copies for overlay phis on normal CFG edges — not wasm branch operands that re-enter typed loop headers.
- `ssa-nomerge` is safe because typed-loop-param HOT mutation still skips via `ssa_nomerge_has_loop_param_control(...)`; the raw loop-target exceptions are separate, limited to direct current-loop backedges recognized before rewrite, and use stack-neutral or edge-local copy placement before the proxy/store lowering updates loop-param scratches.
- Broader typed-loop-param behavior is fail-closed for HOT SSA mutation and regression-covered: pipeline traces must not contain `pass[ssa-nomerge]:mutated` for unsupported typed-loop-param fixtures, locals written before the loop stay preserved, and backedge-carried param values stay separate from unrelated body locals. The older `br_if` fixture-validation blocker is superseded by the current scalar WAT and concrete-ref programmatic mixed-family fixtures; remaining fail-closed cases are multi-result typed loops, non-current `br_table` targets, branch-bearing nested `loop` / `try_table`, and broader loop-param/header SSA shapes.
- Future work requires loop-param-aware liveness, use-def facts for branch operands, phi placement at typed loop headers, rename semantics that distinguish entry vs backedge param values, destruction copies before loop backedge terminators, lowering that preserves typed loop branch operands for the still-unsupported branch/result shapes, and validated coverage for each widened subset — not broad Binaryen parity claims for typed-loop SSA.
- Exceptional-edge SSA remains explicitly unimplemented and intentionally deferred. The CFG already records `ExceptionalEdge` successors for `try` / `try_table` headers and throw-family terminators, but SSA v1 liveness, dominators, phi placement, dominator-stack rename, and predecessor-copy destruction all follow the normal-flow-only contract.
- Catch continuations are not dominated by throwing blocks.
- The current rename algorithm cannot propagate reaching definitions across exceptional edges without a dedicated exceptional SSA mode.
- `ssa-nomerge` is safe because it skips exceptional-flow HOT mutation via `ssa_nomerge_has_exceptional_flow(...)`, not because the local SSA overlay models exceptional successors.
- Exceptional-flow behavior is fail-closed for HOT SSA mutation and regression-covered: `try_table` write-before-throw, default-local catch continuation, conditional throw with a preceding local write, legacy `rethrow` / `delegate` shapes, and a pipeline trace that must not contain `pass[ssa-nomerge]:mutated`. Some existing raw/no-write normalization may still preserve semantics, but `ssa-nomerge` must not enter HOT local-SSA rewriting for exceptional-flow functions. These tests prove preserved local traffic where writes exist; they do not enable exceptional SSA rewriting.
- Full exceptional SSA remains deferred. Future work requires exceptional-inclusive liveness, catch-block phi placement, exceptional phi inputs, rename semantics for catch blocks, SSA destruction copies before throw/rethrow/delegate terminators, and shape-by-shape guard narrowing with rewrite tests — not Binaryen parity claims for exceptional SSA.
- The O4z public preset still intentionally no-ops `ssa-nomerge`; the direct-pass corruption and debris fixes do not by themselves justify re-enabling the O4z slot.
- The 2026-06-09 direct final lane is normalized-green at `99751/100000` with `0` mismatches, and the param-slot / needed-copy follow-ups stayed green at `9977/10000`; artifact exact parity and O4z neighborhood replay remain open.
- The direct `[SSA]001` temp-local declaration drift is closed by focused tests plus the current `10000 / 10000` `gen-valid` lane.
- The focused extracted-function CLI replay now proves that the old `Func 523` `writeback-validate:type mismatch` skip is retired.
- A fresh direct traced skip census after the large-structured / `Func 4302` follow-up is available in `.tmp/ssa-nomerge-high-threshold-narrow-ssa-trace`, and the post-`bcf4b9199` rerun in `.tmp/ssa-nomerge-post-bcf4-trace` had raw fast/no-op skip families `2524` `structured-local-writes`, `1077` `no-local-writes`, `1020` `straight-line-local-writes`, and `17` `large-structured-local-writes`; there were `0` `skip-invalid-lower` lines. The 2026-06-11 `4608`-instruction budget slice updated the large census to `15`; the later `5376` structured budget slice updated it to `11`, and the high-threshold / no-copy `br_table` follow-up updates it to `9` `large-structured-local-writes` with still `0` `skip-invalid-lower` in `.tmp/ssa-nomerge-structured-8192-brtable-trace`; remaining large skips carry exact payloads such as `func=(Func 3781) instrs=39283 locals=6634`. The older `2026-04-11` count of `228` suspicious skips and the param-slot follow-up count of `1` `Func 4302` suspicious skip are both superseded.
- The same input still succeeds under Binaryen with `wasm-opt tests/node/dist/starshine-debug-wasi.wasm --all-features --ssa-nomerge`.
- So the current output-facing blocker for the reduced `Func 523` family is fixed, the `Func 4302` false-positive suspicious skip is narrowed away, most large-structured direct no-ops are now covered, and the high-threshold raw-structured artifact size regression is fixed by needed-only copies/canonical body-local reuse. Direct artifact replay remains mandatory because exact normalized/canonical function parity is not green and the remaining `9` huge structured functions are still skipped.

## Practical Rule

- Keep direct debug-artifact replay in the `ssa-nomerge` signoff loop.
- Treat the seeded `binaryen-rec-group-zero` wasm-smith failure as an oracle parser gap, not an SSA semantic mismatch.
- Treat current-source behavior parity as green for the fixed dead-param family, the reduced unreachable compare-carrier follow-up, the exceptional-edge fail-closed guard, the raw no-write default-local rewrite, the raw no-write dropped-unreachable-debris cleanup, and the raw structured needed-copy/canonical-local cleanup, but do not claim exact artifact parity until a fresh traced full-artifact replay is normalized/canonical-function equal or the remaining representation drift is intentionally accepted.
- Keep the direct artifact replay and the `10000 / 10000` `gen-valid` compare lane together as the minimum signoff pair; the current `0x5eed` `gen-valid` lane is green in `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-10000-post-bcf4` (supersedes `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-10000-if-order-fix-rerun`).
